[30;1m33 | [0m[35m    This implements the ensemble Kalman filter (EnKF). The EnKF uses[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35m    an ensemble of hundreds to thousands of state vectors that are randomly[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35m    sampled around the estimate, and adds perturbations at each update and[0m

[30;1m37 | [0m[35m    in hydrophysics. As such, this class is admittedly a toy as it is far[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35m    too slow with large N.[0m
